<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздравлять.html>поздравля́ть</a> (4892)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здравый.html>здра́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zdrávyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поздравлять.html>поздравля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pozdravljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поздравить.html>поздра́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to congratulate, to felicitate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поздравлять.html>поздравля́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>днём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рождение.html>рожде́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pozdravljáju s dnjóm roždénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">happy birthday!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***позеленеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:позеленеть.html>позелене́ть</a> (18890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зеленеть.html>зелене́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zelenétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позеленеть.html>позелене́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pozelenétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зеленеть.html>зелене́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become green
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:позеленеть.html>позелене́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зависть.html>за́висти</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:ревность.html>ре́вности</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pozelenétʹ</b> ot závisti (révnosti)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn/be green with envy (jealousy)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to grow/turn green</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зеленый.html>зелёный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zeljónyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зелень.html>зе́лень</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zélenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зеленщи́к</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zelenščík</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зазеленеть.html>зазелене́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zazelenétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позиционный.html>позицио́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poziciónnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:позиционный.html>позицио́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poziciónnaja</b> igrá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">positional game <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in chess</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:познавать.html>познава́ть</a> (21634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познать.html>позна́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poznátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познавать.html>познава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poznavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познать.html>позна́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">philosophy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cognize</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:познание.html>позна́ние</a> (6058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познать.html>позна́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poznátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познание.html>позна́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poznánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познание.html>позна́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познание.html>позна́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познание.html>позна́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cognition, perception</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">usually in the plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> experience, knowledge</li></ol>

***познать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:познать.html>позна́ть</a> (7221)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познать.html>позна́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poznátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познавать.html>познава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">philosophy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cognize</li>
<li>to get to know, to learn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:познать.html>позна́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poznátʹ</b> samovó sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">know oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:познать.html>позна́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:природа.html>приро́ды</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:общественный.html>обще́ственного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:развитие.html>разви́тия</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poznátʹ</b> zakóny priródy (obščéstvennovo razvítija)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">learn the laws of nature (social development)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to experience, to get to know
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рано.html>ра́но</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:познать.html>позна́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>го́ре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ráno <b>poznátʹ</b> góre</i> ― <span class="e-translation">get to know grief early in life</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:позолотить.html>позолоти́вший</a> (16445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотить.html>золоти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zolotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позолотить.html>позолоти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pozolotítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотить.html>золоти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to gild
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позолотить.html>позолоти́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пилюля.html>пилю́лю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pozolotítʹ piljúlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> to sweeten the pill; sugar the pill</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позолотить.html>позолоти́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ручка.html>ру́чку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pozolotítʹ rúčku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cross someone's palm with silver, cross someone's hand with silver</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***позор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:позор.html>позо́р</a> (4868)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позор.html>позо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pozór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позор.html>позо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позор.html>позо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позор.html>позо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shame, disgrace, infamy, humiliation
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1886</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Chekhov</a>,  “The Chorus Girl”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасти.html>спасти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нищета.html>нищеты́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:позор.html>позо́ра</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A méždu tem jestʹ srédstvo spastí jevó i nas ot niščetý i <b>pozóra</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And yet there is a chance of saving him and us from destitution and <b>disgrace</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:позорить.html>позо́рить</a> (14443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позор.html>позо́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pozór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
